[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing run for the `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` target fails with a â€œPermission deniedâ€ [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror when attempting to execute the fuzzer binary [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m inside [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer binary exists but is not executable by the current user or the permissions [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The mount flags used by the base-runner imageâ€”check if the volume is mounted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith restrictive `ro` or `noexec` options.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m70[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m61:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Meson build definition for the multi-threaded fuzzer `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoes not include an `install` directive. OSS-Fuzzâ€™s Meson-based build sequence [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelies on `ninja install` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith `[0m[33mDESTDIR[0m[39m=$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to stage built fuzzer binaries into[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`$OUT` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe directory later mounted as `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` in the Docker container[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Without [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`install: true`, Meson never copies the fuzzer into the install tree, so although [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe file appears under the mounted volume, its mode bits are not set to executable [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minside the container, leading to â€œPermission deniedâ€ [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit code [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer itself [0m[1;39m([0m[39mits sources, dependencies, link flags, and threading logic[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains correct; only its install/installation metadata is missing.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Proposed Patch[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Modify the Meson build file `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`, at the [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m, â€¦[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` declaration, to add:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     â€¢ `install: true`[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     â€¢ `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures that during `ninja install` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwith prefix = `$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, Meson will [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstage `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` into `$OUT/bin` with permission mode `[0m[1;36m0755[0m[39m`. When the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOSS-Fuzz runner mounts `$OUT` to `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`, `[0m[35m/out/bin/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` will be [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable by the fuzzing user, eliminating the permission error.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other changes to harness, tests, or external dependencies are required.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build` and locate the `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m70[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Update its definition block from:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          â€¦,[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          build_by_default: true,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      to:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          â€¦,[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          build_by_default: true,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          install: true,[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Re-run the OSS-Fuzz build pipeline [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMeson setup, `ninja`, `ninja install`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Verify in the build-out directory that `build/out/dav1d/bin/dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexists and has mode `-rwxr-xr-x`.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Execute `run_fuzzer dav1d_fuzzer_mt` in the container; confirm that [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/bin/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` is launched without permission errors.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adding the `install` metadata is the standard Meson mechanism to mark binaries[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor staging during `ninja install`, and it preserves execute permissions [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mautomatically.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No existing logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39msource code, fuzzer flags, threading[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is altered, so [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality remains intact.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change is local to Meson build scripts and does not touch harness or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing engine code, satisfying OSS-Fuzz guidelines.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar Meson-based fuzzer projects [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., those in other VideoLAN modules[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minclude exactly this pattern to ensure their binaries are executable in the fuzzing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontainer.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer binary will be installed under `bin/` instead of root of the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstall tree; OSS-Fuzzâ€™s runner automatically discovers it under `$OUT`, so no [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness change is needed.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If any downstream test or script assumed the binary in a different location, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupdate only that referenceâ€”but in our case, the runner mounts the entire install [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprefix, so calls to `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` will resolve to [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/bin/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` transparently if `bin/` is on `$PATH`. If not, a symlink[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcould be added, but in practice OSS-Fuzz scripts search recursively for the fuzzer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure that all other libFuzzer targets in the project also have their [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`install` directives, to avoid similar permission issues in the future.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By marking `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` as an installed Meson executable, we restore the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpected `[0m[1;36m0755[0m[39m` permission under the OSS-Fuzz mount, eliminating the â€œPermission [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeniedâ€ failure without touching harness code or external libraries. This maintains[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuild hygiene and follows the Meson idiom for staging executables.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m70[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m61:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m70[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m61:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The â€œPermission deniedâ€ [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit code [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m occurs because the fuzzing binaries [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`dav1d_fuzzer_mt` and its sibling `dav1d_fuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are built by Meson but never [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstalled into the `$OUT` staging directory with executable permissions.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - OSS-Fuzzâ€™s Meson-based builds expect a `ninja install` step [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor equivalent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopy fuzzers into `$OUT` with +x bits. Without `install: true`, Meson omits these [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutables from its install manifest. However, the container runner mounts the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhostâ€™s build output directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`build/`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` regardless, yielding [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnonâ€executable files at `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Critical Logic  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not alter the fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`run_fuzzer` wrapper, Docker invocation, or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest code[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep existing compiler flags, `build_by_default` settings, and multiâ€threading[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Only modify Meson metadata in `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build` to include [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstallation directives.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Implementation Steps  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the two invocations of `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`:  [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - One for `dav1d_fuzzer` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - One for `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m70[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. For each `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call, add the keyword argument:  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      install: true,[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Optionally you may add `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,` but Mesonâ€™s [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault `bindir` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprefix/bin[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is already appropriate for executables.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. After patch, the `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` block should look like:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```meson[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          link_with: libdav1d,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          build_by_default: true,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          install: true,[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Apply the same `install: true` to the `dav1d_fuzzer` definition above it.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Why This Fix Works  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - With `install: true`, Meson generates an install target that copies the built [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzers into the install prefix [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich, under OSS-Fuzz, is mapped to `$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During the OSS-Fuzz build, after `ninja -C build` the build script runs `ninja[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-C build install`. The fuzzers now appear in `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` with correct mode bits [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`rwx` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor owner[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The Docker runner thus finds `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` executable and can [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuccessfully launch it under libFuzzer.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No impact on existing production tools or runtimes: only test/fuzzer-related [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuild metadata changes.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing CI style checks and Mesonâ€™s `build_by_default` remain unchanged.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing tests remain unmodified; test harnesses are unaffected.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in Codebase  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The pattern mirrors `install: true` used for the main CLI tool in [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tools/meson.build` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m109[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m123[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach is standard across OSS-Fuzz Meson projects: ensure fuzz targets [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclare `install: true`.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m49:e[0m[39mndif[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m51:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:51[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m59[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m51:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m70[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The OSS-Fuzz build infrastructure invokes â€œmeson installâ€ to populate the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`$OUT` directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmounted as `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` in the runner[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with the built fuzz targets.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In tests/libfuzzer/meson.build, the fuzzing executables `dav1d_fuzzer` and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dav1d_fuzzer_mt` are defined with `build_by_default: true` but lack the `install: [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrue` directive. Meson will compile these into the build directory but will not [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstall them to the prefix [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without an explicit `install: true`.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - As a result, when the base-runner mounts the install prefix to `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`, the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpected binaries under `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` either do not exist or exist without[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable permissions, leading to the â€œPermission deniedâ€ [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit code [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m error [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen the fuzzer runner attempts to execute them.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not alter any harness or fuzzer invocation logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`run_fuzzer`, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCMake/Makefile, Docker runner, or test code[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain multi-threaded fuzz configuration [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msanitization flags.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Continue building the executables by default [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`build_by_default: true`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat local developer workflows are unaffected.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Implementation Steps[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Edit tests/libfuzzer/meson.build:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In the `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m, â€¦[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` definition [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mkeyword argument `install: true`.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In the `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m, â€¦[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` definition [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m70[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlikewise add `install: true`.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional but recommended[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Specify `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`install_dir: [0m[32m'.'[0m[39m` to control the install location. Given the OSS-Fuzz default [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMeson prefix is `$OUT`, adding `install_dir: [0m[32m'.'[0m[39m` ensures the fuzzers land directly[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmatching the runnerâ€™s expectation[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Rebuild and install:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Ensure the OSS-Fuzz build steps perform:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         meson setup builddir --[0m[33mprefix[0m[39m=[0m[32m"$OUT"[0m[39m â€¦  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ninja -C builddir  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ninja -C builddir install  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This will copy both `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` into `$OUT` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mcontainer `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with executable bits intact.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adding `install: true` is the standard Meson mechanism to include a target in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `meson install` step. This directly addresses the missing/unenforced executable[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`, eliminating the â€œPermission deniedâ€ error.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No harness, test, or fuzzing logic is modified, preserving existing tests and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer invocations.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach aligns with other Meson-based OSS-Fuzz projects, where fuzz [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargets explicitly opt into installation.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side effect: The binaries will now be installed under `$OUT/bin` if [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`install_dir` is not specified. Since the runner expects them at [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`, ensure `install_dir: [0m[32m'.'[0m[39m` is used.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: Validate installation layout in a local build [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., inspect [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`$OUT` directory[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before submitting. Add a simple CI check to verify the presence [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand executability of `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` and `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[39m`.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in Codebase[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other Meson-based fuzz targets in OSS-Fuzz often include:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'xyz_fuzzer'[0m[39m, â€¦, install: true, install_dir: [0m[32m'.'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This patch mirrors that pattern to maintain consistency.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. No Additional File Retrieval Required[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change is localized to a single build script [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. No other files need updates or inspection.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith these modifications, the fuzzer binaries will be correctly installed with [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable permissions in `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`, and the OSS-Fuzz runner will be able to launch [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand its single-threaded counterpart[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m without encountering [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpermission errors. [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify Root Cause[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer binaries `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` are built by Meson [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut never installed into the OSS-Fuzz output directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`$OUT`, mounted at `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAs a result, the `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` file that ends up being mounted into the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDocker container is stale [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor a zero-byte stub[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and lacks the executable bit, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to a â€œPermission deniedâ€ [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexit code [0m[1;36m126[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before any harness logic runs.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue building both single-threaded and multi-threaded fuzzers with[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same source files, compiler/linker flags, and dependencies.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We should not modify any fuzzing harness, test code, or external scripts; only[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Meson build definitions are in scope.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Strategy[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Modify `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build` to instruct Meson to install the fuzzer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutables into the configured `prefix` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich OSS-Fuzz sets to `$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with their[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecute permission preserved.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. For both `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` targets, add:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `install: true`[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. This ensures that when the OSS-Fuzz build script runs:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        $ meson setup build -[0m[33mDprefix[0m[39m=$OUT [0m[33m...[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        $ ninja -C build[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        $ ninja -C build install[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      the executables end up in `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer[0m[39m*` with the proper +x bits.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Locate the two [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m declarations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m59[0m[39m and ~[0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m70[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Amend each block as follows [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexample for `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang,[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       install: true,[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mirror the same two lines [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`install: true`, `install_dir: [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m into the `dav1d_fuzzer` declaration.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mesonâ€™s `install:` keyword ensures the binary is copied to the installation [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprefix when `ninja install` is invoked.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Specifying `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` places the executable at the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot of `$OUT` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi.e., `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, matching the runnerâ€™s expectation.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The execute permission bit is preserved by Meson during installation, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolving the â€œPermission deniedâ€ error.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The OSS-Fuzz container will now contain the fuzzer binaries in `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malongside any other installed artifacts. This is standard OSS-Fuzz practice.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No existing tests or harness code are modified; they continue invoking [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` as before.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Should any other install targets be missing, they would manifest similarly; a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreview of other `install:` declarations can be done in follow-up patches.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After applying the patch, rebuild OSS-Fuzz locally:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       $ meson setup build -[0m[33mDprefix[0m[39m=$OUT[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       $ ninja -C build[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       $ ninja -C build install[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` exists, is non-zero size, and has `-rwxr-xr-x` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpermissions.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rerun the fuzzer in the Docker runner:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       $ run_fuzzer dav1d_fuzzer_mt -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     and confirm it no longer errors with â€œPermission denied.â€ [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
