[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m165[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mwarning[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'Files larger than 2 gigabytes might not be supported in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mthe dav1d CLI tool.'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m166[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35madd_project_arguments[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'-U_FILE_OFFSET_BITS'[0m[39m, language: [0m[32m'c'[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m167[0m[39m:        elif [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'enable_tools'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m168[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35merror[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d CLI tool needs fseeko[0m[32m([0m[32m)[0m[32m'[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m169[0m[39m:        else[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m170[0m[39m:            have_fseeko = false[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m171[0m[39m:        endif[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m172[0m[39m:    endif[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m173:e[0m[39mndif[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m174[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m175[0m[39m:libdl_dependency = [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m176[0m[39m:if [0m[1;35mhost_machine.system[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m[32m'linux'[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m177[0m[39m:    libdl_dependency = [0m[1;35mcc.find_library[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dl'[0m[39m, required : false[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m178[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;35mcc.has_function[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dlsym'[0m[39m, prefix : [0m[32m'#include <dlfcn.h>'[0m[39m, args : [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest_args, dependencies : libdl_dependency[0m[1;39m)[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m179[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mcdata.set[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'HAVE_DLSYM'[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m180[0m[39m:    endif[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:51[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m59[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m51:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m54[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m55[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests/libfuzzer/meson.buil[0m[1;92md:61[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m70[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m61:da[0m[39mv1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:    include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:    c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:    link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:    link_with : libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:    build_by_default: true,[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:    dependencies : [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:    kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzing runner mounts the projectâ€™s â€œinstall prefixâ€ directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhost [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`build/out/dav1d` â†’ container `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and then invokes `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`. [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBecause the Meson build for the fuzzer executables did not include any `install:` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirective, Meson never copies [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand therefore never marks as executable[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m those [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbinaries into the install prefix. The mount is effectively an empty directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontains non-executable placeholders[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so attempting to exec `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39myields a â€œPermission deniedâ€ [0m[1;39m([0m[39mEACCES[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m error.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Behavior[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to build both `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` by default[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mvia `build_by_default: true`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not touch any harness, test, or Docker logic; the runner and [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer-invocation flags remain unchanged.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We only augment the Meson scripts so that after `ninja install` the fuzzer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbinaries land in the prefix with correct executable permissions.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Outline[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`, locate the two executable definitions:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - The block for `dav1d_fuzzer` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m51[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - The block for `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m61[0m[39mâ€“[0m[1;36m70[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. To each `[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call, add:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `install: true,`[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. This tells Meson to install the built binaries directly into the prefix [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich OSS-Fuzz binds to `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with default install mode [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0755[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, making[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthem immediately executable.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. No other changes are required; `ninja`, followed by `ninja install`, will [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpopulate `[0m[35m/[0m[95mout[0m[39m` with `dav1d_fuzzer` and `dav1d_fuzzer_mt`. The existing [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer-runner invocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m â€¦`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will then succeed.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Detailed Steps[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `tests/libfuzzer/meson.build`.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Modify the `dav1d_fuzzer` definition:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer'[0m[39m,[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_with: libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        build_by_default: true,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install: true,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Modify the `dav1d_fuzzer_mt` definition likewise:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      dav1d_fuzzer_mt = [0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[32m'dav1d_fuzzer_mt'[0m[39m,[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dav1d_fuzzer_sources,[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        include_directories: dav1d_inc_dirs,[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        c_args: [0m[1;39m[[0m[32m'-DDAV1D_MT_FUZZING'[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_args: fuzzer_ldflags,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        link_with: libdav1d,[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        build_by_default: true,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install: true,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        install_dir: [0m[1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'prefix'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        dependencies: [0m[1;39m[[0m[39mthread_dependency[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        kwargs: fuzzer_link_lang[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Rebuild and install:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `meson setup --reconfigure out â€¦` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOSS-Fuzz build system already sets [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`-[0m[33mDprefix[0m[39m=$OUT`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `ninja -C out`[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `ninja -C out install`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Verify inside the Docker runner that `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m` exists and is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecutable:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `ls -l [0m[35m/out/[0m[95mdav1d_fuzzer_mt[0m[39m  # mode should be -rwxr-xr-x`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Re-run `run_fuzzer dav1d_fuzzer_mt â€¦` â†’ should start the fuzzer instead of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPermission denied.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Rationale & Side-Effects[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By leveraging Mesonâ€™s native `install` mechanism, we avoid any manual copy or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpost-build hack, preserving alignment with other project targets.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adding executables to the install prefix is standard practice in OSS-Fuzz [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprojects; it has no negative impact on production installs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe fuzzer binaries are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `--prefix/bin` or root, but tests and production packages ignore them[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change does not alter existing library code, utility functions, or [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness logic, so it is low-risk and reversible.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Future Meson refactors will still install the fuzzers correctly as long as [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`install: true` remains paired with the fuzzer targets.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar pattern is already used for the `dav1d` CLI tool in `meson.build`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich employs `install: true` and an `install_dir`.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Meson manual: â€œ[0m[1;35mexecutable[0m[1;39m([0m[39mâ€¦, install: true, install_dir: [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mget_option[0m[1;39m([0m[32m'bindir'[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mâ€ is the canonical way to ship binaries.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
